msg:The double bed room, room 910, booked on Ctrip for more than 500 yuan, has a bad smell in the bathroom. It is estimated that it is the smell from the toilet or the sewage. This will not be an individual case, it is estimated that a batch of rooms or rooms with this pipeline will have this problem. Such rooms will be released, showing the lack of management. It is recommended that the hotel management and family members live in each room of the hotel, conduct an evaluation, and try to see if such a room can be lived. Due to the bad smell in the bathroom, we had to open the window all afternoon, and the smell was still bad when we slept at night. We slept with the window open all night, and the noise from the cars on the road outside was negligible. This is the first time I encountered such a five-diamond hotel, and it feels like traveling back to 20 years ago. The other aspects of the hotel can be summed up in the phrase "go back to 20 years ago", and it is exactly the same. The hotel is a high-rise in the urban area. It could have seen the cityscape, but half of the windows are corrugated glass, and half of the flat glass is covered with flowers, and the window is only half of the room bay. In the dark and low seating area in the lobby on the first floor, someone was smoking majesticly. Such a hotel is so old that you can travel back to 20 years ago, Ctrip actually says that it will be renovated in 2020. I booked it on Ctrip casually, just took a look at the location and the decoration in 2020, and thought that Ctrip's five diamonds should be no problem. As a result, Ctrip gave me medicine again. It seems that Ctrip should be careful in the future when booking, the rating score is too inconsistent with the reality. If you have the opportunity, please invite Ctrip's management team to come to this hotel with your family to experience it on the spot.
